## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of population change (dP/dt) as a function of time and current population size, which is the core problem in population dynamics. The inclusion of both t and P as features suggests possible non-autonomous dynamics such as time-varying growth rates or carrying capacities.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth common in tumor/biological systems)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (depensation without critical threshold)
- Seasonal Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) (exponential growth with periodic rate modulation)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with time-varying growth rate)
- Time-varying carrying capacity logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P * c1 * (1 + c2 * t)**(-1)) (logistic with linearly increasing capacity)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**(c2)) * c3 (generalized growth model)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (hyperbolic density dependence)
- Exponential decay with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (growth/decline with constant immigration)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth minus proportional harvesting)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional/anomalous growth dynamics)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density dependence in population models тЖТ multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) representing resource limitation
- Allee effects (cooperative dynamics) тЖТ additional multiplicative factor (P - c) or (c + P) creating growth reduction at low densities
- Gompertz-type asymmetry тЖТ log(c/P) term indicates growth rate decreases logarithmically as population approaches capacity
- Seasonal/periodic environmental forcing тЖТ multiplicative modulation by (1 + c*sin(c*t)) or (1 + c*cos(c*t)) on growth rate
- All population growth rates must vanish at P=0 тЖТ dP/dt should contain P as a multiplicative factor (extinction is absorbing state)
- Rational density dependence тЖТ P/(1 + c*P) form indicates contest-type competition rather than scramble competition
- Time-varying capacity or parameters тЖТ explicit t-dependence through polynomial, exponential, or trigonometric functions of t multiplied into autonomous terms
- Multiple equilibria in population models тЖТ polynomial factors in P of degree тЙе 2, e.g., P*(P-c1)*(c2-P) indicating bistability

I need to analyze the GT expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**GT expression:**
`0.845*(-1 + P/5.115)*(1 - P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P`

Let me expand this:

**First term:** `0.845*(-1 + P/5.115)*(1 - P/34.44)*P`

Let me expand `(-1 + P/5.115)*(1 - P/34.44)`:
= `-1 + P/34.44 + P/5.115 - P┬▓/(5.115*34.44)`
= `-1 + P*(1/34.44 + 1/5.115) - P┬▓/176.16`

Multiply by 0.845*P:
= `0.845*(-P + P┬▓*(0.02904 + 0.1955) - P┬│/176.16)`
= `0.845*(-P + 0.2245*P┬▓ - 0.005677*P┬│)`
= `-0.845P + 0.1897P┬▓ - 0.004797P┬│`

**Second term:** `0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P`
= `0.845*P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)`

**Combined GT:**
= `-0.845P + 0.1897P┬▓ - 0.004797P┬│ + 0.845P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)`
= `0.1897P┬▓ - 0.004797P┬│ - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)`

So GT = `c0*P┬│ + c1*P┬▓ + c2*P*exp(c3*P)` where c0 тЙИ -0.004797, c1 тЙИ 0.1897, c2 тЙИ -0.845, c3 тЙИ -0.0969.

Now I need a candidate of the form: `P┬│*a + P┬▓*b + P*c*exp(P*d)` (with possible additive constant = 0).

**Candidate 31:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P + c4`

This is `c0*P┬│ + c1*P┬▓ + c2*P*exp(c3*P) + P + c4`. The extra `+P` term can't be eliminated (it has coefficient 1, fixed). We'd need the linear P term to be 0 in the GT. Since there's no free constant on the `+P` term, this doesn't work.

**Candidate 24:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P + c4*log(P*c5 + 1) + c6`

Same issue with the fixed `+P`.

**Candidate 27:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + c3*exp(P*c4) + c5`

This is `c0*P┬│ + c1*P┬▓ + c2*P + c3*exp(c4*P) + c5`. The GT has `P*exp(...)`, not just `exp(...)`. Not equivalent.

**Candidate 7:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + P*c3 + P + c4`

= `c0*P┬▓ + c1*P*exp(c2*P) + (c3+1)*P + c4`. This has P┬▓ and P*exp but no P┬│. Doesn't match.

**Candidate 30:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P + c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`

Has `exp(P*c3)` not `P*exp(...)`. No match.

**Candidate 2:** `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(P*c2) + P*c3` = `(c0+c3)*P + c1*P*exp(c2*P)`. Missing P┬│ and P┬▓ terms.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
$$f(P) = 0.845(-1 + P/5.115)(1 - P/34.44)P + 0.845(1 - e^{-0.0969P})P$$

Let me expand the first term:
$$(-1 + P/5.115)(1 - P/34.44) = -1 + P/34.44 + P/5.115 - P^2/(5.115 \times 34.44)$$

So the first part times 0.845P:
$$0.845P(-1 + P/34.44 + P/5.115 - P^2/176.16)$$
$$= 0.845(-P + P^2/34.44 + P^2/5.115 - P^3/176.16)$$

The second part: $0.845(P - Pe^{-0.0969P})$

Combining:
$$= 0.845(-P + P^2(1/34.44 + 1/5.115) - P^3/176.16 + P - Pe^{-0.0969P})$$
$$= 0.845(P^2(1/34.44 + 1/5.115) - P^3/176.16 - Pe^{-0.0969P})$$

Computing constants:
- $1/34.44 + 1/5.115 \approx 0.02904 + 0.19550 = 0.22454$
- $P^2$ coefficient: $0.845 \times 0.22454 \approx 0.18974$
- $P^3$ coefficient: $-0.845/176.16 \approx -0.004797$
- Exponential term: $-0.845 \cdot P \cdot e^{-0.0969P}$

So GT = $aP^3 + bP^2 + cPe^{-dP}$ where $a \approx -0.004797$, $b \approx 0.18974$, $c \approx -0.845$, $d \approx 0.0969$.

**Key basis functions in GT:** $P^3$, $P^2$, $Pe^{-dP}$ (with $d > 0$).

Note: There's no constant term, no $P$ term (the linear terms cancelled), and no $t$ dependence.

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 24: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2e^{Pc_3} + P + c_4\log(Pc_5+1) + c_6$

= $P^3c_0 + P^2(c_1+c_2) + P(c_3+c_4) + c_5\log(Pc_6+1)$. Log not equivalent to $Pe^{-dP}$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 27: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + c_3e^{Pc_4} + c_5$
Has $e^{cP}$ not $Pe^{cP}$. These are linearly independent. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 28: $Pc_0 + Pc_1e^{Pc_2} + Pc_3 + Pc_4$
= $P(c_0+c_3+c_4) + Pc_1e^{Pc_2}$. Missing $P^3$, $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 29: Has $t$ in $\cos(c_1 t)$. Setting $c_1=0$: $P^2c_0 + P(c_2+c_3) + c_4\log(P^2c_5+1)$. Missing $P^3$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 30: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + P + c_2e^{Pc_3} + c_4$
Has $e^{cP}$ not $Pe^{cP}$. Also has fixed $+P$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 31: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2e^{Pc_3} + P + c_4$
Has $Pe^{cP}$, $P^3$, $P^2$, $P$, constant. GT = $aP^3 + bP^2 + cPe^{dP}$ (where $d<0$). Can we set $c_4=0$? Then $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2e^{Pc_3} + P$. The extra $+P$ can't be zeroed. But GT has no linear $P$ term. So this doesn't match unless the $+P$ can be absorbed. It can't since $Pe^{cP}$ and $P$ are linearly independent. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 32: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + c_3\log(Pc_4+1) + c_5 + c_6/(Pc_7+c_8)$
Log and rational, no exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 33: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + Pc_3e^{c_4 t}$
Setting $c_4=0$: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + P(c_2+c_3)$. Polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 34: $P^2c_0 + c_1 + c_2\log(Pc_3+1)$
Missing $P^3$, exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 35: $P(c_0+c_1) + Pc_2/(Pc_3+1) + c_4\log(Pc_5+1)$
No $P^3$, $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 36: Has $t$. Setting $c_2=0$: $P(c_0+c_1) + c_4\log(P^2c_5+1)$. Missing $P^3$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 37: Has $t$. Setting $c_4=0$: $P^3c_0 + Pc_1/(Pc_2+1) + c_6$. Missing $P^2$, exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 38: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2/(P+c_3) + c_4$
Rational term, no exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 39: $P^3c_0 + Pc_1 + c_2\log(P^2c_3+Pc_4+1)$
Missing $P^2$, has log. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 40: Has $t$ in sin. Setting $c_4=0$: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + c_3$. Polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 41: $P^3c_0 + P^2(c_1+1) + Pc_2$. Polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 42: $P^3c_0 + P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + c_3\log(Pc_4+1) + c_5\sin(\ldots)$. No exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 43: Has $t$. Setting $c_4=0$ or $c_3=0$: polynomial. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 44: No $P^3$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 45: $P^3c_0 + Pc_1/(Pc_2+1) + P + c_3\log(Pc_4+1)$. No $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 46: Has $t$. Setting $c_5=0$: $Pc_0 + Pc_1e^{Pc_2} + P(c_3+c_4)$. Missing $P^3$, $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 47: $P^3c_0 + P^2(c_1+c_2+c_3) + Pc_4/(P+c_5) + P(c_6+c_7)$. No exponential. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 48: No $P^3$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 49: $P^3c_0 + Pc_1 + Pc_2/(Pc_3+1) + c_4\log(Pc_5+1)$. Missing $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 50: Missing $P^2$. **NO MATCH**

None of the candidates contain the required combination of $P^3$, $P^2$, and $Pe^{cP}$ without extra non-removable terms.
